Other Annotations
Index

Annotations provide names and keywords for Unicode characters, currently focusing on emoji. If you see any problems, please file a ticket with the corrected values for the locale. For the XML data used for these charts, see latest-release annotations or beta annotations. For more information, see LDML Annotations.

This table shows the annotations for a group of related languages (plus English) for easier comparison. The first item is the short name (also the text-to-speech phrase). It is bolded for clarity, and marked with a * for searching on this page. The remaining phrases are keywords (labels), separated by â€œ|â€. The keywords plus the words in the short name are typically used for search and predictive typing.

Most short names and keywords that can be constructed with the mechanism in LDML Annotations are omitted.
